\mbox{\Hypertarget{libmmg2d__private_8h_a53daf9ecb1452fa9bd10c969c1d95d54}\label{libmmg2d__private_8h_a53daf9ecb1452fa9bd10c969c1d95d54}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{lissmet\_ani()}{lissmet\_ani()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int lissmet\+\_\+ani (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a73ac506fe087cc604bb892e46373719a}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Sol}}}]{sol }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer toward the mesh \\
\hline
{\em sol} & pointer toward the metric\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if fail, 1 if success
\end{DoxyReturn}
Anisotropic gradation (h-\/gradation procedure). See\+: \cite{borouchaki1998mesh}. The Hc-\/correction method is used (gradation with respect to H-\/shock measure). Skip edges with a required extremity (treated in lissmetreq\+\_\+ani).

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMG2D\_assignEdge()}{MMG2D\_assignEdge()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int MMG2\+D\+\_\+assign\+Edge (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer toward the mesh\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if fail, 1 otherwise
\end{DoxyReturn}
Transfer some input edge data to the corresponding triangles fields The cleaning of required tags inside triangles has been initially added by commit da4b099c. It probably followed the report of a bug arising when several library functions are successively called without cleaning the mesh structure but on december 2022 I am not able to reproduce this bug. Due to tags cleaning, input required edges are lost in ls discretization mode (see issue \#171). The met\+Ridtyp field (previsouly not used in 2D) is now used to mark if {\itshape MMG2\+D\+\_\+assign\+Edge} function is called for the first time inside the library and if we have to clean triangle tags (in order to fix issue \#171 without breaking again the initial fix).

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMG2D\_boulen()}{MMG2D\_boulen()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int MMG2\+D\+\_\+boulen (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int}]{start,  }\item[{int8\+\_\+t}]{ip,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{pleft,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{pright,  }\item[{double $\ast$}]{nn }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer toward the mesh \\
\hline
{\em start} & index of the first tria \\
\hline
{\em ip} & local index of the point on which we work in tria {\itshape start} \\
\hline
{\em pleft} & index of the left point of ip along the geom edge (local index of the point inside a triangle) \\
\hline
{\em pright} & index of the right point of ip along the geom edge (local index of the point inside a triangle) \\
\hline
{\em nn} & computed normal at ip\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if fail, 1 if success
\end{DoxyReturn}
Travel the ball of point {\itshape ip} in triangle {\itshape start}, which is assumed to lie either on the external or on an internal boundary of the mesh, and return the normal vector convention\+: the normal vector is oriented from the half ball it starts with towards its exterior return pright = 3$\ast$kk+ii, where kk = last triangle in the first travel, and ii = local index of ip in kk pleft = 3$\ast$kk+ii, where kk = last triangle in the second travel, and ii = local index of ip in kk. 

Definition at line \mbox{\hyperlink{boulep__2d_8c_source_l00115}{115}} of file \mbox{\hyperlink{boulep__2d_8c_source}{boulep\+\_\+2d.\+c}}.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily int MMG2\+D\+\_\+defsiz\+\_\+iso (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a73ac506fe087cc604bb892e46373719a}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Sol}}}]{met }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\end{DoxyReturn}
New version for the definition of a size map; takes into account the curvature of the external and internal curves present in the mesh 1) Size at internal points

Step 1\+: Set metric at points belonging to a required edge\+: compute the metric as the mean of the length of the required eges passing through the point

Step 2\+: size at non required internal points

Step 3\+: Minimum size feature imposed by the boundary edges

If local parameters are provided\+: size truncation on the entire mesh

\index{MMG2D\_Free\_all\_var@{MMG2D\_Free\_all\_var}!libmmg2d\_private.h@{libmmg2d\_private.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMG2D\_Free\_all\_var()}{MMG2D\_Free\_all\_var()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int MMG2\+D\+\_\+\+Free\+\_\+all\+\_\+var (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{va\+\_\+list}]{argptr }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em argptr} & list of the mmg structures that must be deallocated. Each structure must follow one of the {\itshape MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG} preprocessor variable that allow to identify it.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
{\itshape argptr} contains at least a pointer toward a {\itshape MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh} structure (that will contain the mesh and identified by the MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+pp\+Mesh keyword)

To call the {\itshape MMG2\+D\+\_\+mmg2dlib} function, you must also provide a pointer toward a {\itshape MMG5\+\_\+p\+Sol} structure (that will contain the ouput metric (and the input one, if provided) and identified by the MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+pp\+Met keyword).

To call the {\itshape MMG2\+D\+\_\+mmg2dls} function, you must also provide a pointer toward a {\itshape MMG5\+\_\+p\+Sol} structure (that will contain the level-\/set function and identified by the MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+pp\+Ls keyword).

To call the {\itshape MMG2\+D\+\_\+mmg2dmov} library, you must also provide a pointer toward a {\itshape MMG5\+\_\+p\+Sol} structure storing the displacement (and identified by the MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+pp\+Disp keyword).

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if fail, 1 if success
\end{DoxyReturn}
Internal function for deallocations before return (taking a va\+\_\+list as argument).

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
we pass the structures by reference in order to have argument compatibility between the library call from a Fortran code and a C code. 
\end{DoxyRemark}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily MMG5\+\_\+int MMG2\+D\+\_\+grad2met\+\_\+ani (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a73ac506fe087cc604bb892e46373719a}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Sol}}}]{met,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a20e63fab5273f15ae1a3cae77bfcdcb6}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Tria}}}]{pt,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int}]{np1,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int}]{np2 }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer toward the mesh \\
\hline
{\em met} & pointer toward the metric \\
\hline
{\em pt} & pointer toward the processed triangle. \\
\hline
{\em np1} & first edge extremity (global index) \\
\hline
{\em np2} & second edge extremity (global index)\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if fail or we don\textquotesingle{}t need to modify the sizes. ier, where (ier \& 1) if metric of {\itshape ip1} is altered, and (ier \& 2) if metric of {\itshape ip2} is altered.
\end{DoxyReturn}
Perform simultaneous reduction of metrics at ip1 points and ip2, and truncate characteristic sizes so that the difference between two corresponding sizes respect the maximal gradation.

Ref \+: \href{https://www.rocq.inria.fr/gamma/Frederic.Alauzet/cours/cea2010_V2.pdf}{\texttt{ https\+://www.\+rocq.\+inria.\+fr/gamma/\+Frederic.\+Alauzet/cours/cea2010\+\_\+\+V2.\+pdf}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMG2D\_hashQuad()}{MMG2D\_hashQuad()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int MMG2\+D\+\_\+hash\+Quad (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer toward the mesh structure.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if failed, 1 otherwise.
\end{DoxyReturn}
Create full table of adjacency for quadrangles (quad $ <-> $ quad adjacencies and quad $ -> $ tri adjacencies)\+: 1) if the edge $ i1 $ of quad $ k1 $ is adja to quad $ k2 $ through edge $ i2 $, $
adja[4*(k1-1)+1+i1] = 4*k2+i2 $. 2) if the edge $ i1 $ of quad $ k1
$ is adja to tria $ k2 $ through edge $ i2 $, $
adja[4*(k1-1)+1+i1] = -(3*k2+i2) $. Step 1\+: Fill adjacendies between quadrangles

Step 2\+: Fill adjacencies between quadrangles and triangles

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMG2D\_Init\_mesh\_var()}{MMG2D\_Init\_mesh\_var()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int MMG2\+D\+\_\+\+Init\+\_\+mesh\+\_\+var (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{va\+\_\+list}]{argptr }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em argptr} & list of the mmg structures that must be initialized. Each structure must follow one of the {\itshape MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG$\ast$} preprocessor variable that allow to identify it.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
{\itshape argptr} contains at least a pointer toward a {\itshape MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh} structure (that will contain the mesh and identified by the MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+pp\+Mesh keyword)

To call the {\itshape MMG2\+D\+\_\+mmg2dlib} function, you must also provide a pointer toward a {\itshape MMG5\+\_\+p\+Sol} structure (that will contain the ouput metric (and the input one, if provided) and identified by the MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+pp\+Met keyword).

To call the {\itshape MMG2\+D\+\_\+mmg2dls} function, you must also provide a pointer toward a {\itshape MMG5\+\_\+p\+Sol} structure (that will contain the level-\/set function and identified by the MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+pp\+Ls keyword).

To call the {\itshape MMG2\+D\+\_\+mmg2dmov} library, you must also provide a pointer toward a {\itshape MMG5\+\_\+p\+Sol} structure storing the displacement (and identified by the MMG5\+\_\+\+ARG\+\_\+pp\+Disp keyword).

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 if fail, 1 otherwise
\end{DoxyReturn}
Internal function for structure allocations (taking a va\+\_\+list argument).

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{MMG2D\_locateEdge()}{MMG2D\_locateEdge()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily int MMG2\+D\+\_\+locate\+Edge (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{libmmgtypes_8h_a906478a19c4819942a0eea48823b774b}{MMG5\+\_\+p\+Mesh}}}]{mesh,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int}]{ia,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int}]{ib,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{kdep,  }\item[{MMG5\+\_\+int $\ast$}]{list }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em mesh} & pointer toward the mesh \\
\hline
{\em ia} & index of first extremity of the edge \\
\hline
{\em ib} & index of second extremity of the edge \\
\hline
{\em kdep} & pointer toward the index of the first element intersecting the edge \\
\hline
{\em list} & pointer toward the list of elts intersected by the edge\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
4 if the edge exist in the mesh, 0 if fail, ??? otherwise
\end{DoxyReturn}
Calculate the list of all the triangles intersected by edge (ia,ib), starting from kdep = one triangle in the ball of ia; {\itshape list} starts at index 0 (and ends at index lon-\/1). It stores 3$\ast$k + iare, where {\itshape k} is an intersected tria and {\itshape iare} is an intersected edge. prod1, prod2 and prod3 allow to localize the edge regarding the tria\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item if all are \texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}0, the edge doesn\textquotesingle{}t cross the tria (same sign for all areas)
\item if 2 are negative and 1 is positive, the edge intersect 2 triangle edges
\item if 2 are 0, the edge pass through 1 of the tria vertices
\item if 3 are 0, the edge coincide with 1 of the tria edges
\end{DoxyItemize}

ia-\/ib intersect 2 triangle edges =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} 2 products are \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}0, 1 is \texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}0

Definition at line \mbox{\hyperlink{locate__2d_8c_source_l00329}{329}} of file \mbox{\hyperlink{locate__2d_8c_source}{locate\+\_\+2d.\+c}}.
